## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
participant Test as EntityStateHistoryTests
participant EDAO as FakeEntityDAO
participant HDAO as FakeEntityStateHistoryDAO
participant Factory as EntityStateHistoryFactory
participant Handler as Handler
participant EntityObj as Entity

Test->>HDAO: add_history(default_entity, delivered)
Test->>HDAO: add_history(default_entity, completed)
Test->>HDAO: add_history(default_entity, archived)
Test->>Factory: new EntityStateHistoryFactory(HDAO, EDAO)
Factory->>Handler: create_handler()
Test->>Handler: handle(request)
Handler-->>Test: result (list[EntityStateHistory])
```
